+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(GEMM_K // 8):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + lane_col
+            if m0 < GEMM_M:
+                batch0 = m0 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial0 = m0 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // OUT_W
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % OUT_W
+                in_channel = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                filter_offset = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                k0 = filter_offset // KERNEL_W
+                k1 = filter_offset % KERNEL_W
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + 32 + lane_col
+            if m1 < GEMM_M:
+                batch1 = m1 // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                spatial1 = m1 % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                out_row1 = spatial1 // OUT_W
+                out_col1 = spatial1 % OUT_W
+                in_channel = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                filter_offset = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                k0 = filter_offset // KERNEL_W
+                k1 = filter_offset % KERNEL_W
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + lane_col
+            if n0 < GEMM_N:
+                in_channel = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                filter_offset = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                k0 = filter_offset // KERNEL_W
+                k1 = filter_offset % KERNEL_W
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < GEMM_N:
+                in_channel = k // (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                filter_offset = k % (KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W)
+                k0 = filter_offset // KERNEL_W
+                k1 = filter_offset % KERNEL_W
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * WARP_TILE_M + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * WARP_TILE_N + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < GEMM_N:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < GEMM_M:
+                        batch = row // (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        spatial = row % (OUT_H * OUT_W)
+                        out_row = spatial // OUT_W
+                        out_col = spatial % OUT_W
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

codex
The compiler limitation is narrower than the algorithm: the JIT is rejecting several kernel-body references to module constants. I’m inlining the numeric tile sizes and GEMM extents inside the kernel body so the AST the MLIR generator sees is fully literal.

+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):

+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+

+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+

+            and x.dtype == torch.float32

+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+

+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+

+                k0 = filter_offset // 9

+                k0 = filter_offset // 9

+

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+            if m0 < 4096512:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // 504
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if m1 < 4096512:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                out_row1 = spatial1 // 504
+                out_col1 = spatial1 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:
+        return (
+            tuple(x.shape) == INPUT0_SHAPE
+            and x.dtype == torch.float32
+            and self.conv2d.in_channels == IN_CHANNELS
+            and self.conv2d.out_channels == OUT_CHANNELS
+            and self._normalized_kernel_size() == (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+            and self.conv2d.stride == (STRIDE, STRIDE)
+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS
+            and self.conv2d.bias is None
+        )

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight.detach()
+        key = (weight.data_ptr(), x.device.type, x.device.index, x.dtype, weight.is_contiguous())
+        if self._weight_cache_key != key:
+            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._weight_cache_key = key

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+            if m0 < 4096512:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // 504
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if m1 < 4096512:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                out_row1 = spatial1 // 504
+                out_col1 = spatial1 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]

-                                    acc += S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.f32) * S.convert(W[oc, ic_local, k0, k1], S.f32)
-                    Y[n, oc, o0, o1] = acc
+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+            if m0 < 4096512:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // 504
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if m1 < 4096512:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                out_row1 = spatial1 // 504
+                out_col1 = spatial1 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:
+        return (
+            tuple(x.shape) == INPUT0_SHAPE
+            and x.dtype == torch.float32
+            and self.conv2d.in_channels == IN_CHANNELS
+            and self.conv2d.out_channels == OUT_CHANNELS
+            and self._normalized_kernel_size() == (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+            and self.conv2d.stride == (STRIDE, STRIDE)
+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS
+            and self.conv2d.bias is None
+        )
 
-    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, kernel_size: int, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, bias: bool = False):
-            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, in_channels, kernel_size, stride=stride, padding=padding, groups=in_channels, bias=bias)
+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight.detach()
+        key = (weight.data_ptr(), x.device.type, x.device.index, x.dtype, weight.is_contiguous())
+        if self._weight_cache_key != key:
+            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._weight_cache_key = key
+        return self._weight_cache
 
-    def forward(self, x):
-        if tuple(x.shape) != (16, 64, 512, 512) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
-            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
+    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        if not self._supports_optimized_path(x):
+            raise RuntimeError(
+                "This optimized kernel only supports input shape "
+                f"{INPUT0_SHAPE}, float32 inputs, and Conv2d("
+                f"{IN_CHANNELS}, {OUT_CHANNELS}, ({KERNEL_H}, {KERNEL_W}), "
+                f"stride={STRIDE}, padding={PADDING}, dilation={DILATION}, groups={GROUPS}, bias=False)."
+            )
         x0 = x.contiguous()
-        w = self.conv2d.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
-        y = torch.empty((16, 64, 510, 510), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
+        w = self._get_cached_weight(x0)
+        y = torch.empty(OUTPUT_SHAPE, device=x0.device, dtype=OUTPUT_TORCH_DTYPE)
         fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
         return y

+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:
+        return (
+            tuple(x.shape) == INPUT0_SHAPE
+            and x.dtype == torch.float32
+            and self.conv2d.in_channels == IN_CHANNELS
+            and self.conv2d.out_channels == OUT_CHANNELS
+            and self._normalized_kernel_size() == (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+            and self.conv2d.stride == (STRIDE, STRIDE)
+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS
+            and self.conv2d.bias is None
+        )

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight.detach()
+        key = (weight.data_ptr(), x.device.type, x.device.index, x.dtype, weight.is_contiguous())
+        if self._weight_cache_key != key:
+            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._weight_cache_key = key
+        return self._weight_cache

         fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
         return y

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),

+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+

    def run(*popenargs,
            input=None, capture_output=False, timeout=None, check=False, **kwargs):
        """Run command with arguments and return a CompletedProcess instance.
    
        The returned instance will have attributes args, returncode, stdout and
        stderr. By default, stdout and stderr are not captured, and those attributes
        will be None. Pass stdout=PIPE and/or stderr=PIPE in order to capture them,
        or pass capture_output=True to capture both.
    
        If check is True and the exit code was non-zero, it raises a
        CalledProcessError. The CalledProcessError object will have the return code
        in the returncode attribute, and output & stderr attributes if those streams
        were captured.
    
        If timeout is given, and the process takes too long, a TimeoutExpired
        exception will be raised.
    
        There is an optional argument "input", allowing you to
        pass bytes or a string to the subprocess's stdin.  If you use this argument
        you may not also use the Popen constructor's "stdin" argument, as
        it will be used internally.
    
        By default, all communication is in bytes, and therefore any "input" should
        be bytes, and the stdout and stderr will be bytes. If in text mode, any
        "input" should be a string, and stdout and stderr will be strings decoded
        according to locale encoding, or by "encoding" if set. Text mode is
        triggered by setting any of text, encoding, errors or universal_newlines.
    
        The other arguments are the same as for the Popen constructor.
        """
        if input is not None:
            if kwargs.get('stdin') is not None:
                raise ValueError('stdin and input arguments may not both be used.')
            kwargs['stdin'] = PIPE
    
        if capture_output:
            if kwargs.get('stdout') is not None or kwargs.get('stderr') is not None:
                raise ValueError('stdout and stderr arguments may not be used '
                                 'with capture_output.')
            kwargs['stdout'] = PIPE
            kwargs['stderr'] = PIPE
    
        with Popen(*popenargs, **kwargs) as process:
            try:
                stdout, stderr = process.communicate(input, timeout=timeout)
            except TimeoutExpired as exc:
                process.kill()
                if _mswindows:
                    # Windows accumulates the output in a single blocking
                    # read() call run on child threads, with the timeout
                    # being done in a join() on those threads.  communicate()
                    # _after_ kill() is required to collect that and add it
                    # to the exception.
                    exc.stdout, exc.stderr = process.communicate()
                else:
                    # POSIX _communicate already populated the output so
                    # far into the TimeoutExpired exception.
                    process.wait()
                raise
            except:  # Including KeyboardInterrupt, communicate handled that.
                process.kill()
                # We don't call process.wait() as .__exit__ does that for us.
                raise
            retcode = process.poll()
            if check and retcode:
>               raise CalledProcessError(retcode, process.args,
                                         output=stdout, stderr=stderr)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import importlib.util
import subprocess
import sys
import unittest
import _substrate_bindings as _C
import torch

from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


ROUND_OUTPUT = "/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p83/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round2/output_model_new.py"


def _load_round_module():
    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("kb_round2_output_model_new", ROUND_OUTPUT)
    if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Unable to load round module from {ROUND_OUTPUT}.")
    module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(module)
    return module


def _generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    del jit_fn
    script = f"""
import importlib.util
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import _build_import_module, _collect_jit_dependencies, _get_function_def

path = {ROUND_OUTPUT!r}
spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("kb_round1_output_model_new_subproc", path)
module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(module)
jit_fn = module.fused_kernel
jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])
generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)
for dep in jit_deps:
    generator.visit_function_def(_get_function_def(dep.parse()), "[]", "jit")
generator.visit_function_def(_get_function_def(jit_fn.parse()), "[]", "kernel")
print(generator.get_mlir())
"""
    return subprocess.check_output([sys.executable, "-c", script], text=True)


@unittest.skipUnless(has_rocm(), "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.")
class TestConv2DAsym(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_weight_cache_reuses_device_tensor_until_storage_changes(self):
        module = _load_round_module()
        model = module.ModelNew(*module.SUPPORTED_INIT_ARGS, stride=1, padding=0, dilation=1, groups=1, bias=False).cuda()
        x = torch.empty(module.INPUT0_SHAPE, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        with torch.no_grad():
            cached0 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            cached1 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            self.assertEqual(cached0.data_ptr(), cached1.data_ptr())

            model.conv2d.weight = torch.nn.Parameter(model.conv2d.weight.detach().clone())
            cached2 = model._get_cached_weight(x)
            self.assertNotEqual(cached1.data_ptr(), cached2.data_ptr())

    def test_kernel_mlir_contains_mfma(self):
        module = _load_round_module()
        mlir = _generate_mlir(module.fused_kernel)
        self.assertIn("mfma", mlir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+            if m0 < 4096512:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // 504
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if m1 < 4096512:
+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032
+                out_row1 = spatial1 // 504
+                out_col1 = spatial1 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n0, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])
+        acc[1, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag0[0], acc[1, 0])
+        acc[1, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], acc[1, 1])
+
+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,

+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)

+    for tm in S.range(2):
+        for tn in S.range(2):
+            tile_row_base = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + tm * 32
+            tile_col_base = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + tn * 32
+            col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+            if col < 64:
+                for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+                    row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)
+                    if row < 4096512:
+                        batch = row // 256032
+                        spatial = row % 256032
+                        out_row = spatial // 504
+                        out_col = spatial % 504
+                        Y[batch, col, out_row, out_col] = acc[tm, tn, acc_idx]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:

+            tuple(x.shape) == INPUT0_SHAPE
+            and x.dtype == torch.float32
+            and self.conv2d.in_channels == IN_CHANNELS

+            and self.conv2d.stride == (STRIDE, STRIDE)
+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+        if self._weight_cache_key != key:
+            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):

+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):
+        a_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+        b_words = S.full((2, 2), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        a_frag1 = S.view(a_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k = k_tile * 8 + lane_k_base + e
+
+            m0 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + lane_col
+            if m0 < 4096512:
+                batch0 = m0 // 256032
+                spatial0 = m0 % 256032
+                out_row0 = spatial0 // 504
+                out_col0 = spatial0 % 504
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch0, in_channel, out_row0 + k0, out_col0 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            m1 = group_m_base + warp_row * 64 + 32 + lane_col

+                batch1 = m1 // 256032
+                spatial1 = m1 % 256032

+                out_col1 = spatial1 % 504

+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col
+            if n0 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9

+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col
+            if n1 < 64:
+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(W[n1, in_channel, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:
+        return (
+            tuple(x.shape) == INPUT0_SHAPE
+            and x.dtype == torch.float32
+            and self.conv2d.in_channels == IN_CHANNELS
+            and self.conv2d.out_channels == OUT_CHANNELS
+            and self._normalized_kernel_size() == (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+            and self.conv2d.stride == (STRIDE, STRIDE)
+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS
+            and self.conv2d.bias is None

+    def _get_cached_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:

+            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),

+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64

+    warp_col = warp % 2

+            return kernel_size

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((16, 32, 512, 512), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((64, 32, 5, 9), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((16, 64, 508, 504), S.f32),
+):
+    lane = S.thread_id(0) % 64
+    warp = S.thread_id(0) // 64
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    group_m_base = S.block_id(1) * 128
+    group_n_base = S.block_id(0) * 128
+    lane_col = lane % 32
+    lane_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+    acc = S.full((2, 2, 16), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(180):

+        b_frag0 = S.view(b_words[0], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        b_frag1 = S.view(b_words[1], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

+                filter_offset = k % 45
+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9

+                k0 = filter_offset // 9
+                k1 = filter_offset % 9
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(X[batch1, in_channel, out_row1 + k0, out_col1 + k1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                a_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+            n0 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + lane_col

+            else:
+                b_frag0[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)

+            n1 = group_n_base + warp_col * 64 + 32 + lane_col

+                in_channel = k // 45
+                filter_offset = k % 45

+                k1 = filter_offset % 9

+            else:
+                b_frag1[0, e, 0] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc[0, 0] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], acc[0, 0])
+        acc[0, 1] = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag1[0], acc[0, 1])

 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups=1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(
+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._weight_cache = None
+        self._weight_cache_key = None
+
+    def _normalized_kernel_size(self):
+        kernel_size = self.conv2d.kernel_size
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, tuple):
+            return kernel_size
+        return (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+
+    def _supports_optimized_path(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> bool:
+        return (

+            and x.dtype == torch.float32

+            and self.conv2d.padding == (PADDING, PADDING)
+            and self.conv2d.dilation == (DILATION, DILATION)
+            and self.conv2d.groups == GROUPS
+            and self.conv2d.bias is None
+        )
